Domestic Important News

Recent Political News from the Northeast 74

Issuance of Silver Dollar Exchange Notes

Decision to Expand Artillery by Three Regiments

Shenyang Correspondence: The Northeast Political Affairs Committee recently received a telegram from the Central Government ordering an investigation into the following items. The committee immediately forwarded the order to various provinces on the 14th to investigate and report so that it could be compiled and reported to the Central Government. The investigation items are: (1) The vastness and area of the three northeastern provinces and the boundaries bordering Japan and Russia. (2) The total number of mountains, rivers, and waterways in the province. (3) The total number of acres of land owned by the public and private people in the province. (4) The revenue from land taxation and miscellaneous taxes in the province. (5) The finances of the province's military salaries, administrative expenses, public and private budgets, and final accounts. (6) The exact number of people in the province, as well as the nationalities and occupations of foreigners residing in the province. (7) The names of the counties in the province and the distribution of their jurisdictions. (8) The total number of schools in the province and the number of students. (9) The police administration and the number of police officers in the province.

The Liaoning Provincial Government, realizing that the province's finances were extremely tight and the market was sluggish, and understanding that this was due to the insufficient amount of currency in circulation, believed that it was necessary to issue silver dollar exchange notes to change the situation. It ordered the Three Eastern Provinces Official Bank to quickly find a solution. The bank then replied that it would temporarily issue 10 million yuan of silver dollar notes, fully redeemable, and then lend them to the market to facilitate circulation. The provincial government approved this and reported it to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee for record. Currently, the Official Bank believes that the market situation is becoming increasingly tight, and as the new grain comes to market, there is an even greater sense that the existing banknotes are insufficient for circulation, resulting in a lack of development in trade. Therefore, in accordance with the previously determined method, it has prepared a fund of 10 million yuan and is now raising 5 million yuan as a 100% reserve to issue 5 million yuan of banknotes to relieve the market.

The newly appointed artillery commander, Jin Jingqing, believes that the existing artillery in the Northeast is insufficient for distribution. It is now proposed to expand it by three regiments. Liu Fusheng has been appointed as the commander of the First Regiment, Zhang Sigong as the commander of the Second Regiment, and Zhu Lihan as the commander of the Third Regiment. It is expected that the formation will be completed next month. The junior officers will be filled by graduates of the Artillery Research Class of the Military Academy. After the formation is completed, the First and Second Regiments will be stationed in Jilin and Heilongjiang, respectively, while the Third Regiment will be stationed in the Pingjin area.

For the convenience of command, the military authorities have specially compiled all armored vehicles into a large team, with one commander and one deputy commander each, for a total of four trains. Each train has one squad leader, four platoon leaders, and 360 soldiers, carrying 16 armored vehicles. Each train also has five sections in charge of engineering, communications, design, transportation, etc. Currently, the First Armored Train is on the PingSui Railway, the Second Armored Train is on the PingHan Railway, and the defense areas of the Third and Fourth Armored Trains are unknown. After the Northeast Army entered the customs, many personnel from the various halls and offices of the Border Defense Commissioner's Office were transferred, resulting in a large number of vacancies in the various offices of the Border Defense Commissioner's Office, which has caused a sense of uneven workload. The various directors have requested instructions from Rong Zhen, the military director. It has now been stipulated that temporary transfers will be allowed, such as when Office A is busy and the officers are insufficient, personnel from Office B will be temporarily transferred, and when Office C is busy, personnel from Office D will be temporarily transferred. It has been decided that the vacant officer positions will remain vacant and not be filled because the reorganization of the Border Defense Commissioner's Office is imminent (15th).

Jiangxi Province's Ji'an and Xiajiang Have Been Recovered 75

Chongren Has Also Been Recovered

Relief Association Prepares Relief for Disaster Areas

Nanchang Correspondence: Since Lu Diping arrived in Zhangshu on the 13th, he ordered the First and Second Columns, with Xu Kexiang's division in charge of the frontal attack on Xiajiang along the Gan River. Zhang Huizan's division's Dai Wang Zhu three brigades and Tan Daoyuan's Luo brigade were to pursue the bandits from the east bank of the Gan River, Xingan Chongren. Deng Ying's division [blank space in original text] was also in charge of bandit suppression in Fuzhou. Furthermore, he ordered the Third Column, Luo Lin's division, to attack Ji'an from Fenyi around Anfu, and Gong Bingfan's division from Xinyu Xiajiang to attack the east of Ji'an. The two sides launched a pincer attack. Gong's division and Wang's brigade entered Renhexu, Xiajiang on the 16th, and the division headquarters entered Jiebu on the evening of the 16th. There were only a little over a thousand communist bandits in Xia County, so on the 17th at noon, they captured Xiajiang County and continued to advance towards Ji'an. On the 18th, they joined Luo's division and occupied Ji'an County at 4 p.m. Huang Gonglue and Liu Zuoshu's bandit troops, numbering over 10,000 with approximately 2,000-3,000 rifles, were routed towards Yongxin Xingguo, extremely embarrassed. The provincial government received a telephone call from the Ninth Route Army Headquarters' forward command post in Zhangshu this afternoon (18th) reporting: (1) Xiajiang has been recovered, and the communist bandits on the east and west banks of the Gan River have been routed. Many have been captured by the government army. (2) Ji'an County has been occupied, and the various bandit factions of Huang and Liu have fled, suffering countless casualties and injuries. They are currently being pursued. The provincial government received Ji'an as an important town in western Jiangxi, which was captured by communist bandits on October 4th. They have been burning, killing, looting, and pillaging for a month and a half. Approximately thousands of people have died, and approximately hundreds of houses have been destroyed. The essence of the entire county has been lost. This is truly an unprecedented disaster.

As for the Zhu Mao factions, after Zhang and Tan's divisions resisted and pursued them in Fuzhou, they detoured east towards Fujian. Most of them are currently in the Shicheng Nancheng Ningdu area, only a hundred miles or so from the Fujian border. After Zhang's division recaptured Chongren, the Wang, Dai, and Zhu three brigades all reached Chongcheng and are currently joining Deng's division to pursue towards Yihuang Jianchang. Mao Bingwen's division is also marching towards Fuzhou from the province and should arrive in Fuzhou tomorrow or the day after. In the future, the suppression of the communist bandits on the Shicheng Fujian border will be based in Fuzhou. Therefore, Deng Ying has recently been ordered to rush to build an airfield in Fuzhou, to be completed within three days, so that the aviation team can fly from Fuzhou to the Fujian border to bomb the bandits.

The Fang Zhimin faction in northeastern Jiangxi retreated from northern Jiangxi and occupied Fuliang and Dexing, then moved towards Leping Yiyang. The 55th Division's Ruan Zhaochang's troops have arrived in Fuliang from Wuyuan, Anhui. The 5th Division's Hu Zuyu's brigade has also arrived in Duchang Raoxun from Pengze. After deployment, they will launch a large-scale pincer attack in the hope of wiping them out in one fell swoop. The Provincial Relief Association, considering that more than 60 of the 81 counties in the province have been ravaged by bandits, suffering massacres, the destruction of houses, the loss of homes, and displacement, and that the weather is gradually turning cold and winter is approaching, believes that if relief is not organized quickly, there will be no survivors left. Therefore, it has compiled a statistical report on the bandit disaster situation in the 42 counties, including Yiyang Shanggao, for which investigations have been completed, and has submitted it to the Central Government for overall relief to provide assistance (November 18).

He Jian Reports Hunan Province's Military Expenses Difficulties 76

Education Funds, etc., Have All Been Diverted

Currently, More Than Three Million Yuan is Still Owed

Changsha Correspondence: Hunan Province's military expenses have always relied on Hunan Province's national tax revenue. Usually, the national tax revenue is around one million yuan per month. The military expenditure, excluding temporary expenses, requires a monthly expenditure of one million three hundred to forty thousand yuan. Therefore, previous arrears were often temporarily covered by the provincial treasury to maintain it. According to Finance Director Zhang Kailian's report, from July to the end of October, a further 1,175,795 yuan was advanced from the field tax and unified tax items for military expenses. More than three million yuan advanced before July has not yet been allocated by the central government, causing the provincial treasury to be in a very difficult situation due to the impact of the advances. Recently, due to the spread of banditry, the revenue from national and local taxes has greatly decreased. It is estimated that the national tax revenue in June was only 540,027 yuan and 3 jiao. In July, it was 390,806 yuan and 9 jiao and 4 fen. In August, it was 668,526 yuan and 8 jiao and 2 fen.

Page 9

Domestic News

In September, it was 384,794 yuan. In October, it was 740,450 yuan. In total, the five months of June, July, August, September and October collected more than 2,726,850 yuan. A total of 2,526,446 yuan and 2 jiao and 2 fen were paid for military expenses. According to the monthly military expenditure of 1,340,000 yuan, plus temporary expenses, the total for five months is more than 7 million yuan. Now, only more than 2.5 million yuan has been paid, leaving a shortfall of more than 5 million yuan. At that time, military needs were urgent and there was no way to raise funds. In addition to withdrawing more than 1.17 million yuan from the provincial tax items, the education fund, disaster relief funds, and special commercial loans totaling 1.4 million yuan were completely borrowed. However, the balance between revenue and expenditure still leaves a shortfall of more than 3 million yuan, resulting in the failure to pay more than 600,000 yuan in military expenses in June and the full amount of military salaries in July, August, September, and October. In addition, the provincial treasury's revenue has been greatly reduced due to the unrest caused by bandits. It is estimated that only 60% of the administrative expenses were paid in June, none in July, and only food expenses were maintained in August, September, and October. According to the Finance Department's announcement, a total of 1,649,078 yuan in administrative expenses were owed for June, July, August, September, and October. It is difficult to take care of oneself, let alone have the energy to subsidize military expenses. Therefore, Hunan's finances have reached the point of exhaustion. Wang Jiading, the director of the Finance Department of the Fourth Route Army Headquarters, resigned because he could not find a solution. The directors of the Finance Departments of the 15th, 16th, 19th, and 31st Divisions and the Independent 7th Brigade jointly visited Zhang Kailian, the Director of Finance, yesterday to request a solution. However, in reality, the provincial treasury had no way to help. He Jian was very anxious about this situation. In addition to sending another telegram to the Central Government requesting to resign from his concurrent positions as Commander-in-Chief of the Fourth Route Army, Chairman of the Hunan Provincial Government, Commander of the Hunan Pacification Command, and member of the Hunan Provincial Party Department, he also submitted a memorial to General Commander Chiang requesting assistance in the difficult situation of military expenses in Hunan Province. The memorial is as follows: (Your subordinate has been fighting against the rebels and bandits for two years. The military expenses required have always been taken from the national tax revenue of Hunan Province, which is usually not enough. However, since the two invasions of the Gui rebels and the Communist bandits, the tax revenue in various places has become even more depleted. In the past, counties in western Hunan could be expected to remit taxes monthly to supplement the revenue. Recently, He Kuang fled south, and Nanhua and Jin Feng were also ravaged. There is no time for pacification, so I dare not count on urging the collection of taxes. According to my subordinate's calculation, the current number of troops is about 80,000, and the monthly salary requirement is more than 1.4 million yuan. In addition, the various temporary expenses such as equipment replenishment, straw shoes, and rice subsidies are not included. Based on the current national tax revenue, the monthly revenue is at most only 700,000 yuan. It is uncertain whether this amount can be maintained regularly. Even if it is fortunate to have this amount, it is only enough to pay for food. In terms of salary, there is a difference of more than half. Therefore, the salaries of my subordinate's officers and soldiers have been in arrears for as long as four months. Previously, when the war was at its most intense, a total of 1.4 million yuan was allocated from the Hunan Provincial Education Fund, the Hunan Disaster Relief Fund, and special commercial loans to barely raise the salaries for May and July. As for the 650,000 yuan owed in June and the 700,000 yuan owed in each of August, September, and October, totaling 3 million yuan, there is no way to raise it. Every time I think of the officers and soldiers enduring the hardships of bullets and shells and the difficulties of saving for their livelihoods, I am extremely anxious. According to the current situation, if no urgent measures are taken to remedy the situation, I am afraid that the arrears will become deeper and the difficulties will become greater. Even the item of food is currently extremely difficult, and the future is uncertain. The impact on the pacification will be even deeper and greater. In our Central Government's overall planning, the situation in Hunan Province is naturally well understood. Your subordinate is awaiting punishment in the military and only wants to barely manage and should try his best to economize and never dare to burden the Central Government with financial difficulties. However, the fact is that it is difficult to cook without rice. I have repeatedly requested that all of Hunan Province's special taxes be temporarily allocated for use in Hunan Province to relieve the immediate urgency. This is the reason why the national and local taxes of Hunan Province have already been divided, and the administrative expenses, party expenses, and education expenses are in the same difficult situation. Not only is there nothing to divert, but the 1.4 million yuan previously allocated must be returned urgently. Your subordinate is in this difficult situation and dare not conceal it from the higher authorities. I earnestly beg you to understand this difficult situation and quickly grant relief. I am overwhelmed with anxiety and gratitude.)

Jinan Telephone Company's Appeal Judgment 77

Permission to Revoke Provisional Execution

Jinan Communication: The case of Ma Guanhe, the former general manager of Jinan Telephone Company, privately borrowing 420,000 Japanese yen from the Japanese Dongtuo Company, the Jinan District Court ordered the telephone company to repay the Dongtuo Company's loan and ruled for provisional execution. The telephone company refused to accept the judgment and appealed to the Shandong Higher Court, requesting the revocation of provisional execution. Yesterday, the court ruled to allow the revocation of provisional execution. The telephone communication in Jinan City will not fall into the hands of the Japanese for the time being. As for the telephone company's denial of repaying the loan on behalf of Ma Guanhe, it has also appealed to the Higher Court. The judgment revoking the provisional execution is recorded below:

Shandong Higher Court Civil Second Instance Judgment No. 35 of the 19th Year, Original Text. Appellant: Jinan Telephone Company, Legal Representative Han Chunyi, Litigation Agents Yan Chenghan (Lawyer), Jia Rongqing (Lawyer). Appellee: Toyo Takushoku Kabushiki Kaisha, Legal Representative Kagawa Masao, Litigation Agent Yoshida Kanu, two parties involved in a case of provisional execution. The appellant refused to accept the first instance judgment made by the Jinan District Court on October 3 of this year and filed an appeal. After trial by this court, the judgment is as follows: (Main Text: (The part of the original judgment regarding provisional execution is revoked. The appellee's request for provisional execution in the original trial is rejected. The litigation costs of the second trial shall be borne by the appellee. (Facts) The Japanese Toyo Takushoku Kabushiki Kaisha filed a lawsuit in the original trial against the defendants Ma Guanhe and Jinan Telephone Company, seeking compensation of 420,000 Japanese yen in principal and interest on various loans from the date of the debt until the end of the execution. The original trial ordered the defendants to jointly and severally repay the aforementioned principal and interest and declared provisional execution. Jinan Telephone Company declared its dissatisfaction with the entire original judgment and, in accordance with the provisions of Article 523 of the Civil Procedure Law, requested that the appeal regarding provisional execution be tried first. After this court held a hearing on the provisional execution part on a scheduled date, the appellee was legally summoned but was late for the oral argument date and did not arrive. In accordance with Article 457, Paragraph 1 of the same law, a judgment shall be made. (Reasons) The appellant's argument briefly states that this case is a monetary debt and there is no reason why it cannot be calculated. Regardless of whether Ma Guanhe is still wealthy, even considering the company itself, it has original assets of more than 1.6 million yuan. As certified by the accountant's audit, this year's continued investment is even more than 360,000 yuan, totaling more than 2 million yuan. Although there are other debts of 100,000 yuan, the assets still exceed the appellee's debt amount by a large margin. Although the machinery and equipment are worn out, it cannot be suddenly reduced to the point where it is difficult to offset. Furthermore, the company is engaged in telecommunications and transportation services. If the provisional execution affects the intangible losses or prevents the restoration of the original state, how difficult would it be to calculate the compensation problem in the future? The original judgment declaring provisional execution is inappropriate in both fact and law. Article 463, Paragraph 1 of the Civil Procedure Law stipulates that if the creditor explains that there is a risk of suffering damages that are difficult to offset or difficult to calculate before the judgment is final, the court shall declare provisional execution upon its request. This article stipulates that it is difficult to offset, not insufficient to pay off. Furthermore, this case is a monetary debt with a fixed price that can be calculated, so there is no problem of difficulty in calculation. The original judgment still relied on the appellee's request, pointing to the appellant's property depreciating over time and not being presented for repayment of the debt as difficult to offset, and stating that the economic situation in society and the fluctuation of gold prices were uncertain as difficult to calculate, and hastily declared provisional execution. This is extremely inappropriate. Furthermore, if provisional execution is actually implemented in this case, the appellant's business will inevitably be suspended or other obstacles will occur, and it will inevitably suffer losses that cannot be recovered in the future. According to Article 464, Paragraph 1 of the same law (If the debtor explains that there is a risk of suffering irreparable damage due to provisional execution, if it is the situation in Article 462, the court shall declare that provisional execution is not allowed upon its request. If it is the situation in the previous article, the creditor's request shall be rejected), the appellee's request for provisional execution should also be rejected. Based on the above conclusions, the appeal in this case should be deemed reasonable. In accordance with Articles 518 and 97 of the same law, the judgment is specially made as in the main text. Presiding Judge of the Second Civil Division of the Shandong Higher Court: Yu Jianshu, Judge Yi Xin, Judge Ding Yikui, November 17, 19th Year of the Republic of China. This document is certified to be identical to the original. Clerk Yan Huaqi, November 18, 19th Year of the Republic of China.

Conflict Between Liu's Army and the Militia in Pingdu 78

More Than 500 Civilian Houses Were Burned

More Than 30 Villagers Died

Qingdao Correspondence: The original infantry regiment of Liu Zhennian's troops stationed in Pingdu had previously clashed with the local militia due to an incident. After mediation by various parties, they had been at peace for several months. Unexpectedly, last night (13th), the troops stationed in Liu's army suddenly clashed again with the Tinglanqiu militia, resulting in a tragic death toll and the arrest of more than 100 farmers. Previously, Tinglanqiu in the southwest of Pingdu was the most prosperous area in the county. It had a self-defense militia with sufficient guns and ammunition, with more than 60 militiamen. The militia commander, Liu Desheng, had previously served as an army battalion commander and had always been at odds with Liu's army stationed in Pingdu. Someone reported that Liu Desheng had illegal activities in the village. Liu's army hated Liu Desheng's stubbornness and knew that his weapons were sophisticated, and repeatedly wanted to seize them for their own use. Therefore, they used the pretext of a meeting to trick Liu into the city and detain him. Then, on the night of the 13th, they dispatched about 300 soldiers to surround Tinglanqiu on all sides, launching an attack on one side and setting fire to the four gates on the other. The militia had no leadership and was in an isolated position. After a long and bitter battle, their ammunition was running out. The militiamen knew they could not resist and fled out of the encirclement in the middle of the night. Liu's army did not dare to pursue them deeply and rushed into the village. At that time, flames rose from all sides, burning down most of the village. The cries of women and children were unbearable to hear. After the incident, it was investigated that more than 500 houses were burned down, and about 30 men, women, old and young were burned and shot to death. Countless people were injured. Before leaving, Liu's army also took more than 100 farmers to Pingdu City for detention. How to deal with them is still unknown. After the incident, the Pingdu County Magistrate reported the situation to Commander Liu Zhennian in Yantai and Chairman Han Fuju in Jinan. Commander Liu immediately sent personnel to the scene of the incident to investigate the truth and will deal with the matter impartially to appease public anger and uphold military discipline. It is also heard that the gentry in the county convened a temporary meeting the day before yesterday to discuss how to deal with the aftermath in order to find ways to comfort the victims and resolved to jointly request Commander Liu to release all the farmers who were taken away to show leniency (November 15).

Instructions: To order compliance with matters. It is investigated that the general headquarters of the militia in various parts of the province have reported that they have been organized and should be reviewed to verify the situation. The deputy commander is hereby dispatched to lead four candidates waiting for assignment to the various departments for review one by one. This order is hereby issued.

Regulations: Article 1: All soldiers transferred from various county militias to the general headquarters for organization shall be subject to this regulation for review. Article 2: Reviewers shall handle matters in accordance with the methods specified in this regulation and shall not be perfunctory or negligent. Article 3: Reviewers shall be impartial when reviewing soldiers in various departments and shall not be involved in any personal opinions that may cause abuses. Article 4: Upon arrival at each department, the reviewers shall conduct the following examinations one by one: (A) Whether the name, age, and origin match the register; (B) Whether the background, occupation, and experience are virtuous; (C) Whether the volunteers are suitable; (D) Whether the speech and spirit are sound. Article 5: When reviewers review soldiers in various departments, those with one of the following conditions shall be dismissed: (1) Those with soft bones; (2) Those with epilepsy, dementia, and mental illness; (3) Those with incomplete vision and hearing; (4) Those with physical disabilities and hidden diseases; (5) Those who are local ruffians and hooligans; (6) Those with bad habits and counter-revolutionary activities. Article 6: After reviewing the soldiers in each department, the reviewers shall ascertain the types and numbers of guns and bullets in each department and report them in a list. Article 7: This regulation shall be implemented on the date of promulgation (17th).

Preparing to Open Business Tax: The Finance Department's regulations on opening business tax for stores in various counties in the province have been announced and personnel have been sent to various counties to open it. This county has been commissioned by the Provincial Department to appoint Cheng Jingchuan to meet in Songjiang with the county's Finance and Taxation Bureaus to set up an office in the Finance Bureau to prepare for the opening. It is heard that the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, Zhou Heyun, was invited yesterday to discuss the method of implementation so that it can be held on a regular basis.

Wang Zuoliang Declared Not Guilty: Wang Zuoliang, a gentry from Ganyu County, was previously accused of providing 480,000 yuan in military pay to a certain warlord for counter-revolutionary activities. Suzhou City Telephone Fee Allowed to Be Exempted from Addition: The Suzhou City telephone fee was increased by one yuan per month starting on September 1. The original plan was to add another yuan one month later. Now, after Director Zhao repeatedly reported to the Ministry and discussed it together, the Ministry ordered that the addition be temporarily suspended.

Xuanmiao Temple's Screen Wall Allowed to Be Demolished: The dispute over the issue of preserving and demolishing the Xuanmiao Temple's screen wall has been going on for many months, causing general shops to complain endlessly. Wuxi 86

Double Plank Bridge Robbers Commit Robbery In the area of Shuangbanqiao (Double Plank Bridge), at the border of the Eleventh District (Nanyan Township) and the Twelfth District (Taibo Township) of Wuxi, there is a Tainan Elementary School that has been established for over ten years. The school was founded by Yang Jichen, who is from Jinxiang in Nanyan Township and is currently the head of that township. The school currently has over fifty students. The principal is Yin Weixin, and the teacher is Bo Liang. The school servant, Cao Tingda, joined the school this spring at the age of fifty-one. He is from Xueyan Bridge. The other evening, Principal Yin and the teacher went to the home of Yang Jichen, a nearby school board member, to discuss opening a branch school. Only Cao Tingda was left at the school to guard the door. After the meeting, Yin and the others returned to the school late at night, around 2:00 AM. To their surprise, they found the school gate wide open and three or four bamboo poles lying beside it. Realizing something had happened, they rushed inside and found Cao Tingda lying on Teacher Gong's bed with a bullet hole in his forehead, the bed covered in blood. He was barely breathing and unconscious. The room was in disarray. Realizing that the school had been robbed, they checked for losses. They found that Principal Yin's suitcase, containing clothes and books, and five yuan in cash had been stolen, as well as Teacher Gong's bag, containing several items of clothing. Cao Tingda, having been severely wounded, died at 9:00 AM yesterday. At 4:00 PM, Principal Yin came to the city to report the incident to the county government, requesting an investigation into the countryside this morning to apprehend the thieves and recover the stolen goods.

Labor Schools Run Out of Funds, All Classes Suspended The five labor schools in and around the city of Wuxi have been open for over three years. Over a thousand children of laborers have received an education, with remarkable and commendable results. However, the schools do not charge tuition, and all expenses are covered by the labor union on a monthly basis, averaging 500 yuan per month. This semester, it has been four months since the start of school, and the labor union has not provided any funds, accumulating a debt of 2,000 yuan. The principals and teachers of the schools are unable to continue operating, and they were forced to suspend all classes yesterday (the 20th). As a result, the children of laborers are once again deprived of education.

Another Coincidence of Suicide by Opium Smoking In recent years, suicide cases have frequently occurred in society, mostly due to economic pressure and frustration. Unexpectedly, there was news of another coincidence of suicide by opium smoking yesterday. (1) A Jiangbei migrant, Hui A'da, 31 years old, currently resides at No. 29 Changan Bridge outside the North Gate of this city. He works as a bathhouse attendant. His wife, Xuan, has given birth to a son and a daughter. In the past, A'da had an affair with Jiang A'rong, a woman from nearby Nanjian Hill. Their love grew stronger over time. Recently, A'rong suddenly found another lover and saw A'da as a thorn in her side. Affected by this, A'da inexplicably had an argument with his wife yesterday. He suddenly became weary of life and bought one yuan's worth of raw opium at 2:00 PM, which he secretly smoked to kill himself. It was not until the evening that his wife, Xuan, noticed and rushed him to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. However, due to the excessive amount of poison, his life is in great danger. (2) Wang Heming, a resident of Gandeli near Dongxin Road outside Guangfu Gate, is also from Jiangbei and loves gambling. He always loses when he gambles, and is heavily in debt, unable to repay it. Yesterday, he secretly smoked raw opium in an attempt to commit suicide. After being discovered by his family, he was rushed to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. It is reported that he is out of danger.

Ministry of Education Orders Public and Private Universities to Report Organizational Structures and Staffing 100

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education instructed each university and the education departments and bureaus of each province and city to order provincial and registered private universities to submit their organizational charters in accordance with the order. The order stated: "The investigation of the organizational structures and staffing of each university should comply with the 'University Organization Law' and the 'University Regulations', and amendments should be made in accordance with the Ministry's Order No. 1151 issued in August of the 18th year. However, over the past year, some have submitted amended charters to the Ministry for filing, some have responded that they will comply, and some have not submitted any response. This disparity is insufficient for assessment and supervision. This order reiterates the previous order. All schools, regardless of whether they have filed amendments, should submit their amended organizational structure charters for review. The order should be followed."

Overview of Education in Huai'an County 102

Jin Yingyuan, a local education investigator from the Joint Office for the Preparation of Compulsory Education in Jiangsu Province, recently completed an investigation of education in Huai'an County. The following is an excerpt of the overview:

In recent years, the state of education in Huai'an County has entered a period of stability. Director Wei Lin has governed in an orderly manner, and his efforts in reorganizing and increasing funding have been quite effective. Since taking office, he has been able to issue funds on a monthly basis without any arrears. The internal organization and all facilities of the bureau have been restored to their former state. As a result, the staff of each school can focus on teaching, and the content has gradually improved. All application forms are printed and distributed by the Education Bureau, making the administration more consistent. The budget for the 19th year has already been established. New projects in general education include the establishment of kindergartens, public natural science laboratories, and the addition of higher-level compulsory education in Zhangyang Elementary School. In addition to establishing ten more schools, five levels (eleven levels in total) will be added. In social education, a public education experimental zone will be added (Cheqiao). In addition, the salaries of elementary school teachers will be increased by 70 yuan per grade (18th year), 150 yuan per grade (this year), and 220 yuan per grade (this year). Those with a salary of less than 500 yuan will have their salaries increased to that amount. This will have a significant impact on the future development of education in the county. Various statistics for this year have been compiled successively, which shows the spirit of the Education Bureau's work.

(1) Funding: The budget for the 19th year has already been established. The income includes 111,957 yuan from surtaxes and levies, 4280 yuan from miscellaneous taxes and surtaxes, 4696 yuan from special donations, 490 yuan from miscellaneous donations, 11,490 yuan from property, 3542 yuan from tuition and lodging fees, and 60 yuan from supplementary funds, for a total of 136,542 yuan. The expenditures include 14,718 yuan for education administration, 32,214 yuan for general education, 54,050 yuan for compulsory education, 24,714 yuan for social education, 41,129 yuan for special expenses, and the first reserve fund for the year. Because the budget income for this year is listed based on the actual amount collected, the figures are not complete and have not been included.

(2) Compulsory Education: The entire county is divided into six districts, with a population of 670,967. Of the children of school age, 7,357 are enrolled in schools and 94,816 are not. There are 106 primary schools with 154 levels, occupying 17,161 yuan. There are 125 private schools with 1,828 students. This year, a simple primary school will be piloted in the city, with 97 students divided into two levels and two classrooms. The two levels will be taught, and one level will rotate to another location for work. In the future, if the number of students increases, there will be three levels of classes in one classroom each day, which will be more economical. The county-run middle school has a normal school department with 75 students in the first and second years. Tuition is not charged, and the students receive the same treatment as the students in the middle school department. Two classes have graduated and are serving in elementary schools in the county. When compulsory education is promoted in the future, it seems appropriate to move it to rural areas so that the spirit can be focused and the graduates can serve the rural areas. There are a total of 219 teachers in the county. Nineteen have graduated from normal schools and senior high normal schools, 95 have graduated from county normal schools, 15 have graduated from normal training courses, three have graduated from one-year normal schools, 26 have graduated from the old system middle schools and higher-level middle schools, and nine have passed examinations. It is found that a small number of unqualified teachers are still employed in the county. In the future, the method of promotion will involve increasing the land tax by 6.6% to provide relief and gradually adding simple primary schools to provide relief to those who have dropped out of school. It is suggested to open a teachers' association or correspondence course to increase new knowledge. The existing compulsory education funds will be used for new projects, amounting to 54,050 yuan. There are no accumulated savings (to be continued).

Confucius Temple to Become Cultural Center of the City 103

Municipal Music Hall, Library, and Museum to be Established In addition to using part of the city's Confucius Temple for the Municipal Minglun Elementary School, the remaining buildings will be preserved and may not be used for other purposes. However, due to years of disrepair, the buildings are becoming increasingly dilapidated. It has been reported that the Education and Public Works Bureaus plan to comprehensively renovate the entire Confucius Temple to preserve the historical site and build libraries, music halls, museums, zoos, and other facilities on the surrounding open spaces. To ensure uniform architecture, the new buildings will be generally similar in appearance to the Confucius Temple, making them extremely grand and elegant. This will enable citizens to learn from the ancient sites while also having a place to improve their virtue and rest. Yesterday afternoon, Director Xu of the Education Bureau, Section Chief Li, Director Shen of the Public Works Bureau, Section Chiefs Xue and Huang, and Consultant Dong visited the site to conduct a detailed survey. It was decided that the Public Works Bureau would draft a plan as soon as possible, and after the two bureaus make a decision, a contractor will be hired. The western district is a school area. In the future, after the construction of the various halls is completed, the Confucius Temple will become the cultural center of the city.

The attendees were Wu Jingqing (deputized by Shen Yanong), chief of the First District, Peng Tang, chief of the Second District, Yang Fulin, chief of the Third District, Bi Huan, chief of the Fourth District, Ge Xiusheng, chief of the Fifth District, Wang Chengyao, chief of the Sixth District, Director Shi, Niu Changlian, Lin Qing, and Zheng Guozhai. Director Shi presided, and Pan Shengsan recorded the minutes. After the formalities, the following items were reported: (1) Results of the previous meeting. (2) Recent educational conditions in each district. (3) Overview of the budget for the 18th year. (4) Excerpts from official documents. (5) Holding regular academic competitions for schools in each district. Then the discussion began. (1) The proposal that village elementary schools should hire nearby village chiefs as education promotion and property protection officers was approved in principle. After the measures are drafted, the bureau will submit them to the next meeting for discussion. (2) The proposal that the bureau should submit the budget of a village elementary school to the district office for review when applying for temporary funds, so as to distinguish between urgent and non-urgent needs and to ensure verification, was resolved that the bureau should deliberate and handle the matter in accordance with the original proposal. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Student Petition to Retain President Ma at China Public School 108

Urgent Plea for Professors to Resume Classes

Students at China Public School, concerned that the prolonged absence of certain professors, such as Gao Yihan and Sun Bo [ ], exceeding a month, is significantly hindering their studies, have dispatched a delegation of student representatives with an urgent letter. The petition to the board of directors and the letter to the professors are transcribed below:

Joint Petition to the Board of Directors: Reiterate Previous Request for Rescinding the Approval of President Ma's Resignation and Investigating the Masterminds Behind the Recent Uprising

Regarding our plea to your esteemed council to rescind the approval of President Ma's resignation, the entire student delegation has submitted a request for your review, which has been pending for quite some time without a concrete response. The entire student body is in a state of anxious anticipation. This is because unscrupulous and wicked individuals (such as Ding [ ] Yin) have exhausted their deceptive tactics and engaged in malicious rumors. Recently, they have incited the morally bankrupt elements Li [ ], Yan Jingzhao, and others to instigate a small minority of students to form an illegal organization called the "China Public School Academic Crisis Resolution Alliance," engaging in disruptive activities. Furthermore, School Board Member Mr. You Ren declared upon visiting the school that he lacked the time and energy to serve as president. Therefore, to express the unanimous will of the entire student body to retain President Ma and urge your esteemed council to convene a meeting to resolve this matter promptly, we have reluctantly resolved to initiate a strike. Subsequently, School Board Members Yun and Hu Shi brought a letter from President Ma himself to persuade the students to resume classes. At the time, we were deeply moved by the sincere entreaties of President Ma and Board Members Hu and Wang, who demonstrated genuine concern for our well-being. We reluctantly resumed classes, awaiting a resolution. However, several days have passed since the resumption of classes, and your esteemed council has not yet convened a meeting to rescind the approval of President Ma's resignation. This leaves us in a state of profound doubt, and it appears that our resumption of classes was misguided and failed to adequately express the entire student body's enthusiasm for supporting President Ma and protecting the school to your esteemed council. In order to achieve our objectives, we are compelled to prepare for a second strike to demonstrate our unwavering commitment to upholding [ ].

We believe that your esteemed council members possess even greater sincerity than us, and we trust that you have gained a clear understanding of the rights and wrongs of this uprising. The situation at the school is causing anxiety and chaos among students and staff, and it is teetering on the brink of collapse. Only your esteemed council can rectify the situation and prevent the school from crumbling. We are compelled to reiterate our request and present our final demand. We implore your esteemed council to consider our plea, convene a meeting promptly, rescind the approval of President Ma's resignation, and investigate the masterminds behind this uprising, such as Ding [ ] Yin, revoking Ding's school [ ] qualifications, removing him from his duties as secretary, and restoring fairness [ ] and [ ] the school's foundation. We await your decision with utmost urgency. Respectfully submitted to Chairman Cai of the China Public School Board of Directors.

Letter to the Professors:

Since the outbreak of this unrest, our group has consistently prioritized the valuable time of all students and made sacrifices for their sake. Therefore, from the outset of the unrest, we have strenuously urged students to remain calm and urged professors to attend their classes. We visited the board of directors three times, hoping they would listen to the collective will of all students. However, we repeatedly ignored the expansion of the unrest. Furthermore, morally bankrupt students and their henchmen spared no effort in spreading rumors and creating chaos. The future of our entire student body appeared bleak, forcing us to engage in a three-day strike, a loss that has not been seen in years. This is truly regrettable. Later, we followed the advice of President Ma and Executive Board Members Hu and Wang and reluctantly resumed classes. President Ma immediately sent letters to all professors, requesting that they return to the school to teach. These are undeniable facts. However, you, esteemed professors, have disregarded our intentions and have inexplicably been absent from classes for over a month. You have neither proactively sought a replacement nor requested the registrar to hire capable individuals. You are treating the studies that all students value as child's play. The students have already suffered significant losses. Can you, esteemed professors, truly claim to have a clear conscience? Moreover, the responsibility of a professor is merely to teach, and the right of a student is merely to study. Your actions, esteemed professors, constitute an abandonment of your responsibilities and an infringement upon the rights of others. There is no greater disservice to students than this. We hope that you, esteemed professors, will carefully reconsider your actions and immediately return to the school to resume your classes. Otherwise, for the sake of the interests of the students, our group will have no choice but to request that the school authorities hire replacements. Do not say that we did not warn you. Respectfully, the China Public School Student Delegation.

Sports

Record of Xiqing Basketball Game Yesterday 113

There are three games tonight.

There were three games in the Xiqing basketball game last night. The strength of each side was limited, so the games were quite interesting. There are three games tonight, two in Group A and one in Group B, starting at 7:00.

(1) Jiangwan Beats Laoda (Group A) 114

In one fell swoop, Jiangwan, the pseudonym of the Fudan University basketball team, is one of the new teams in Group A this year. Yesterday, in their first match, they defeated Laoda with a score of 41 to 26. It is hoped that they will be able to win a place in the championship. In the first five minutes of the game, neither side performed well. It was not until Guan Jinlin made a free throw and Zhang Jinxiang followed up with a long shot that Yang Shufan of Laoda also raised his arms and threw in a goal. Jiangwan's three forwards were agile and often attacked, but they missed many shots. Otherwise, the score would have increased greatly. Afterwards, Wu of Jiangwan and Wang of Laoda each scored a goal, making the score six to four. Jiangwan took the lead. At this time, Jiangwan suddenly advanced and scored three goals in the blink of an eye, gaining momentum.

Efforts to Counterattack 115

Laoda's attack failed, and they immediately stopped to discuss tactics and try to counterattack. Song Jinhai took the lead, followed by Zeng Wang, making the score twelve to eight, very close. At this time, Laoda's forward momentum was very strong, and there was a possibility of reversing the defeat. However, because the shots were inaccurate, they still succumbed to Jiangwan. The first half ended with Laoda trailing by twelve to nineteen.

Serious Situation 116

At the beginning of the second half, Laoda's team was greatly strengthened and scored two consecutive goals. Zhang Jinxiang of Jiangwan scored a long shot to boost the spirit of the whole team and regain the lead. The score difference was about ten points. However, after 31 to 20, Laoda had a resurgence of vigor, reaching 31 to 26. The overall trend showed that Laoda was turning the tide.

The Military's Heart is Stabilized 117

Guan Jinlin made a sudden shot, and Zhang, Wu, and Mo scored one after another. Thus, Jiangwan's score was higher. Jiangwan had the victory in hand, and the military's heart was stabilized. Finally, Guan Jinlin scored another goal, adding icing to the cake. As a result, they won with a score of 41 to 26. Referee: Bo La Tuo.

(2) Law School Beats Jiyong (Group B1) 118

The silver flute [ ] Jiyong courageously advanced. Luo Zhaojiong took the lead. Luo's skills were good, and he made several consecutive free throws. Huang Juying, center of Shanghai Law School, first made a free throw and then threw it in. The score between the two sides was very close. In the first half, Jiyong scored eight points and the Law School scored seven points. In the second half, the Law School improved greatly with the addition of Liu Peichang. Within seven minutes, they turned the tide and took a ten to eight lead. Jiyong worked hard to catch up, and the score was close again. After that, the changes were always within one point. The final result was that the Law School won with a score of 19 to 16. Referee: Luo Xunna.

(3) Yuezhong Beats Nanying (Group B2) 119

Yuezhong took the lead, scoring repeatedly, leading by five to two and eleven to five. Nanying then adjusted its troops, and the atmosphere gradually improved. Before long, the score was tied at eleven. Yuezhong's Tie Depeng's goal allowed them to take a thirteen to eleven lead in the first half. In the second battle, the South [ ] was energetic and leaped forward, taking a twenty to seventeen lead. In this critical situation, Yuezhong was fortunate to rely on Cheng Jingxing's two goals to turn the tide. After that, they were invincible and scored every time. As a result, they won with a score of 33 to 20.

Free Talk

Dismissed with a Laugh 123

—Hai Ke

Fiancé—My love, my love for you is truly passionate to the extreme!

Fiancée—Darling, what would you do without me?

Fiancé—Then I can save some on everything.

Diner (to waiter)—Why does this dish taste different today?

Waiter—This is a special dish, so it has a special flavor.

Diner—That’s great, but what is it made of?

Waiter—Things that weren't sold yesterday.

Wife—Why are you nagging incessantly?

Husband—I have important things to say to you, and you have to listen carefully.

Wife—I'm used to hearing you talk in your sleep, but now I have no time to listen.

A (boastfully)—I am a great lover.

B—How great?

A—Just like Valentino and John Gilbert on the screen, women have to fall in love with me.

B—Don't brag, give me an example to see.

A—Just see how many women are heartbroken by disappointment when I get married.

B—So you've married several wives who are heartbroken by disappointment because they married you by mistake?

A Joyful Banquet Between Canadian and Chinese Merchants 124

—Sun Choucheng

The Canadian trade delegation's visit to Shanghai has been valued by all parties. This newspaper has published a special issue to carry news about this item. However, due to space constraints, trivial matters cannot be included. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce hosted a public banquet to welcome the delegation on the second day of their arrival in Shanghai, and I also went there. Therefore, I have a more accurate understanding of what I heard and saw. I would like to add the following details that were not included in the news reports:

The time for the joyful banquet was set at 7:30 PM. Chrysanthemums were placed all over the sides of the escalators, and the national flags of China and Canada were crossed at the entrance. The interior was covered with red carpets. The venue was in the regular meeting room across from the reception room, where the half-length portrait of the Prime Minister was placed. On the four walls were six triangular welcome flags with blue backgrounds and white characters in both Chinese and Western languages. The seats were arranged in a mountain shape, and the tables were filled with chrysanthemums and covered with white carpets. The dishes were contracted by Xinghualou. Each guest had a specially printed five-color hard paper menu with gold lettering measuring three inches wide and six inches long, detailing the names of nine dishes, two snacks, and four fruits, also listed in both Chinese and Western languages. The cutlery and plates were very beautiful. In order to promote domestic products, the banquet was a large-scale Chinese style banquet, and the cigarettes and wine were all products of Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company and Changyu Pioneer Wine Company. Among the Canadian merchants, there were six female guests. Four of them wore black clothes, one wore gray, and the other wore bright red, which was very eye-catching. The guests were divided into two-thirds Chinese and one-half in gowns. Mr. Wang Xiaolai sat in the middle of the chairman's seat, with the head of the delegation, Yemuli, on the left and a female guest in a black coat with a white leather collar on the right. Xie Fusheng sat opposite Chairman Wang, with two Canadian merchants on either side. Because they usually eat with knives and forks and chopsticks are the only ones they have ever seen in their lives, there were many jokes about not knowing how to use them. Sometimes, the Chinese next to them would teach them how to use chopsticks. Those who were clever would try to use them and their satisfied expression would be shown on their faces. Those who were slow to learn would try repeatedly without success, their faces would turn red, and they would laugh loudly. The female guest in red had trouble getting the chopsticks to obey her commands, so she ordered the servant to add knives and forks. The most difficult dish to eat with chopsticks was Yifu noodles. Even after trying dozens of times, the noodles and chopsticks still could not connect, so she abandoned the chopsticks and changed to a fork and magnetic spoon. It took her several tens of minutes to eat a few noodles. It was also difficult. When the wine was half drunk, Wang Xiaolai stood up to give a welcome speech, which was written in white folded paper and read in segments. Xie Fusheng translated each segment, detailing the unequal treatment of Canadian government restrictions on Chinese immigrants and factory exclusions of Chinese workers, and put forward two requirements: (1) Canada should not specially establish immigration laws for China, (2) Merchants should be allowed to come and go freely. Please understand our sincere attitude and earnest wishes and tell the Canadian authorities and all the people to abolish the immigration law against China and sign a reciprocal commercial treaty with our country. The two thousand-plus words were very straightforward. Then, Yemuli gave a reply speech, in addition to expressing his gratitude, he agreed to report to the country on the two requirements and agreed to Chairman Wang's frankness in revealing commercial obstacles for reference and requested that this speech be translated into English and printed in thousands of copies for distribution to the public after returning home so that Canadian merchants who have not been to China can learn about the Chinese psychology. It lasted for forty minutes and was also translated by Mr. Xie. During the informal conversation, the three gentlemen Zhao Jinqing, Yuan Ludeng, and Zhu Yinjiang were the most fluent in Chinese. The three gentlemen Zhao, Yuan, and Zhu had a good foundation in English and could talk directly without the need for a translator. At half past ten, Wang Xiaolai and Xie Fusheng wanted to take the night train to Beijing, so they left first. Before leaving, in addition to cupping his hands in apology, he asked Yuan Ludeng to act as chairman. At a little over eleven o'clock, the photography was finished and the banquet was over.

Talk About the Titles of Presidents 125

—Fei Wenbao

The Republic of China was founded, and the president changed six times. The first president was Mr. Sun Yat-sen. As the poem says, "High mountains are looked up to, and great deeds are followed." Although this mountain has collapsed for a long time, the people's hearts of admiration have never stopped. The successors were Xiangcheng, Huangpi, Hewen, and Donghai. The so-called Cheng, Pei, He, and Hai have already felt that things are getting worse and worse. They have not been restored to the palace, so they have been ordered by Cao Kun. Shan is the thing under the sea. Comparing with the mountains is no different from the three lights in the nine springs. The qualifications of the six presidents gradually coincided with the meaning of the name, and the gradual decline in the middle was in an orderly manner, without the slightest confusion, as if it were made by heaven. This is also an anecdote in the history of the Republic of China. (But reward)

Qing Shuang Sword of the Lihzi Society 126

—Aya sent from Nanjing

Cheng Yushuang came to the capital at the invitation of Mr. Li Shizeng to perform at the Liaoxi Relief Art Fair. She arrived in the capital on the morning of the 13th. Mr. Shu Shifu, Director of the General Affairs Bureau of the National Government's Military Counselor's Office, and officials of the Art Fair took care of everything when they got off the train. She stayed at the Anle Hotel. Recently, because the Northeast generals had just arrived in the capital, nine out of ten hotels were full. Anle was pre-booked, so she was still calm. On the evening of the 14th, Yan Qiu and others performed Qing Shuang Sword at the Lihzi Society. Chairman Jiang and his wife issued invitations in their names, inviting the Northeast generals, ambassadors from various countries, the diplomatic corps, and family members of officials above the rank of Jianren in various institutions. Those without invitations were not allowed to enter. The order was extremely strict. At around 8:00, when the ancient music of the Datong Society was played, only Mr. Zhang Jingjiang and Mr. Wu Zhihui were in the first ten rows. After Mr. Degian and Mrs. Wang Shaolou's "Second Entry to the Palace" came out, Chairman Jiang and Deputy Commander Zhang entered the room from the lounge one after another. The ambassadors of various corps and the officials entered in single file. At a little after 9:00, Yan Qiu's Qing Shuang Sword took the stage. Mayor Zhang Yuejun and Mr. Wu Tiecheng were the first to applaud, and the applause was thunderous. In the cave room scene, after getting the enemy drunk, she bent her bow and drew her sword to assassinate him. When she sacrificed at the tomb, she sang and walked. The audience was deeply moved and explained in detail, as if they were all nodding in agreement and savoring the fun. The theater could accommodate about three or four hundred people. The stage was transformed from a lecture stage. Although the sound was like a short distance behind the twentieth row, it was probably because there were acoustics experts arranged for the lecture. All the scenes were blocked by screens on the side of the stage. The people who inspected the theater were all dressed in the same long gown. Because there were hundreds of foreign guests that day, I was afraid that it would hinder the viewing. After the play, Jiang invited Yan Qiu to join the tea party. The next day, he asked Huang Renlin, the director of the Lihzi Society, to go to Yushuang's place to express his fatigue and pay his respects.

Trivial Records of the Chrysanthemum Banquet 127

—Zheng Yimei

The Chrysanthemum Exhibition has announced its end. Ms. Yu Danhan specially invited Shanghai's prominent calligraphers, painters, and literati to a banquet at the Municipal Hall on the last day. I also participated in the banquet to celebrate the evening. I would like to record the following trivial details:

There are hundreds of thousands of kinds of chrysanthemums, which are extremely elegant, floating in jade, golden in color, and fragrant. There are flowers as big as a bowl, half purple and half white, which are especially beautiful. There is also one flower per pot and one flower per stem, without leaving any other branches and leaves, which is called the Japanese chrysanthemum method. In fact, this method has already existed in our country in the old days, which is called plucking the stamens. Late autumn has not ruined the three paths. Having this in the hustle and bustle of Shanghai is enough to cleanse the viscera.

The calligraphy and painting exhibition displays almost everything. Zhang Shanzi's Twelve Jin钗 is titled with lyrics from the Romance of the West Chamber, but in fact, all the paintings are of Yin beasts, which is a unique opening. Qian Yunhe's Eighteen Arhats Crossing the Sea is a white-line drawing without color, delicate and unparalleled. It was purchased by Wang Xiaolai. The Ding Gaoshan Ju Shi Tu is even more elegant and divine, and is a proud work of the pen. Ms. Yu Danhan's Autumn Sound Map is elegant and pleasant. Several painted fans, Qingxi Fan Zhuo, are added with inscriptions by Zeng Nong Lao, which are especially valuable. Other works such as Ma Mengrong's Quail, Wang Taomin's Crabapple and Banana, Sun Xueni's Landscape, and Zheng Wuchang's Ink Vegetables are all worth appreciating.

Before entering the seat, the painters wrote flower and bird sketches on the long scroll as a unique signature. Then, Ms. Danhan was eager to invite guests to watch the dance and drink wine, and the music was endless. When the wine was half drunk, Qian Shoutie, Sun Xueni, He Tianjian and others gave speeches one after another, planning to organize a large-scale calligraphy and painting exhibition with perfect facilities, and also taking into account the welfare of calligraphers and painters after their deaths, which is a good deed. The banquet ended at ten o'clock.

Travel Notes from Southeast Asia (78) 128

— Linghua

On the tenth, I traveled with Li Zhongqian, the principal of the Zhinan Normal School. Suddenly, an airship appeared in the sky. Li said, "This ship is worth 15,000 yuan and is privately purchased by capitalists for sightseeing. If you want to ride as a passenger, it costs one yuan per minute." If you calculate it this way, an hour costs sixty yuan, equivalent to more than one hundred and thirty yuan in Chinese currency. Such an hour of amusement is quite a spectacle. I once heard from an aviator that a small airship costs no more than 10,000 yuan in China. However, if it becomes popular in the future, the price will surely drop to several thousand yuan, like today's automobiles. Several people could share a ship. However, today, the rich fly in the sky while the poor work in underground cellars. The difference is truly like heaven and earth. Can this system last long? As for the so-called educators, that is, the gentlemen and scholars, they were once the leaders of the four classes of people and teachers of others. Now, they barely make a living and run around the homes of the wealthy to seek a full meal. What value remains in their educational beliefs? Therefore, the children of wealthy families often look down on teachers. The dignity of today's teachers has also been swept away. In this situation, if we want to uphold the ancient virtues of propriety, justice, integrity, and honor, as well as human relations and morality, and the teachings of respect for teachers and the Way, who will follow them?"

Han scholars once said, "The rich become licentious and commit crimes, while the poor become destitute and resort to theft. Their harm is the same." Here, gamblers at horse races use one hundred yuan as a chip, with a minimum bet of five hundred yuan per race, equivalent to over a thousand yuan in Chinese currency. Yet, in the northwest of the mainland, disaster victims cannot even get enough to eat. How can such injustice in the world be tolerated?

Penang Island has magnificent mountains and beautiful scenery, making it a famous scenic area in Southeast Asia. Therefore, all capitalists like to build villas here, making it a gathering place for the wealthy. Having cleverly acquired property, they build secluded retreats to live out their days, far from people and detached from all worldly affairs. This is a well-considered plan. It is said that there are also many wealthy people on Gulangyu Island in China. Some say that Gulangyu Island is the wealthiest of all places, and wealthy people are also sending money there to build villas.

On the thirteenth, I suffered from a fever and eye disease due to the recent heat. Across the street was a hospital run by Taoist Wang. Visiting him, I found out that he was a Taoist from Yuntai Mountain in Haizhou, Jiangsu, and a fellow Shandong native. We had a great connection. He gave me eye drops, which felt very good, but the condition did not improve after a long time. It seems there are many traveling healers in Southeast Asia who use Buddhism or Taoism as a front, selling medicine and various things. It is said that some of them often make a fortune.

From the 24th of the month, my eye disease has not improved, and I have been doing nothing. So, I went to Yangon, accompanied by Yang Shuanglin and Chen Youjia, also known as the monk Yitong. As soon as we boarded the ship, there was wind and rain, and I felt dizzy and vomited for three days and couldn't get up. On the morning of the 27th, we arrived in Yangon. During the journey, I only managed to write four lines of poetry:

Penang west, Shanghai vast and boundless,

Far from my homeland, near the land of Buddha.

Three nights of waves, weary and reluctant,

Once I rejoice in seeing the Great Golden Light (the Great Golden Pagoda).

Warmth in the Heart (319) 129

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 15: In the Private Room, Tears of Melancholy Over Red Love; In the Audience, Hearts Captivated by Lingering Green Charm

Green Charm sat next to Zuo Shichen. Her eyes were still on A Su, who was performing a new patron's song. She seemed uncomfortable, her eyes fixed on A Su, like a chick clinging to its mother. Even though A Su was sitting opposite her, she noticed this. Zuo Shichen held her small hand, as white as snow and as soft as cotton, asking her about everything. Although Green Charm didn't withdraw her hand, she felt shy and only smiled at A Su. A Su had no choice but to join the conversation, saying, "Second Young Master Zuo, you must come and call for her often in the future. Don't be a Danyang visitor." Zuo Shichen asked Green Charm how old she was. Green Charm looked at A Su again. A Su replied for her, "Fifteen years old. We tell other patrons she's sixteen. But it doesn't matter telling the true age to people like the Fourth Young Master and Second Young Master." This song truly took an unusually long time. When Ling Zhixiang's first set of friends had left, and the second set hadn't arrived yet, they came to join the discussion. Everyone said that she was a rising star who would definitely be victorious in the future. They also praised her hair, eyes, and nose. When they hadn't looked at Zuo Shichen's side, they hadn't heard him speak. Now that they had been sitting for a long time, the shy mood that had just settled over them gradually dissipated. When asked what she was saying, she no longer looked at her A Su as if she were a nursemaid. However, when she spoke, there was a delicate sound, like a canary singing, or a clear and round bell. This was something that Rui Yun didn't have. It was just that her vivacity was far inferior to Rui Yun's. Everyone in the room saw that Zuo Shichen treated all the ladies he called casually, but he seemed completely focused and very nervous about Green Charm, this little girl. They couldn't help but be a little surprised. It just so happened that A Su was clinging to her and wouldn't leave. Green Charm followed her instructions, so she didn't dare to move without her permission. Everyone exchanged glances, meaning that Zuo Shichen was under a spell again. But they didn't know if it was well-intentioned or malicious. They were eagerly encouraging the two of them to be intimate. A Su asked, "Fourth Young Master, where are you having dinner tomorrow?" Long Ziyun said, "It hasn't been decided yet." Ling Zhixiang said, "Second Young Master Zuo should treat. Since we have such a good singer, where should we have dinner tomorrow?" Zuo Shichen said, "I'll definitely treat tomorrow. Where would you like to go?" Lin Fanzi said, "The guest follows the host's lead. Wherever you say is fine. We are (the five viscera, willing to follow the whip)." Zuo Shichen said, "If everyone isn't tired of Yuebinlou, we can go there again. Otherwise, a Sichuan restaurant would be good, but I'm afraid of spicy food." Long Ziyun said, "Let's just stay here. It's good to eat familiar dishes. Their business has been really good these days. Let's book a table now." After A Su and Green Charm left, their friends deliberately said, "Green Charm is really good. Green Charm is really not bad."

No matter what, it can only be considered as surplus in terms of physical goods and cannot be said to be worthless. Although it is currently cheaper than domestic prices, the added shipping costs are not negligible. Therefore, if there are no special circumstances in the future, it may be temporarily stabilized. As a result, this month improved by 0.02 yuan compared to the previous day, December improved by 0.0175 yuan, January improved by 0.015 yuan, February improved by 0.01 yuan, and March and April improved by 0.015 yuan.

Speech by representative of the Ministry

Oath of all committee members

The full committee of the China General Federation of Industries held an oath-taking ceremony at the Bankers' Association on Hong Kong Road yesterday. The details are as follows:

Number of attendees: Zhao Jinqing, Director of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, Lin Genghou, Chairman of the National Chamber of Commerce Federation, and committee members Dai Gengxin, Wu Yunchu, Cai Shengbo, Qian Xuanqing, Nie Yisheng, Liu Hongsheng, Qian Chengxu, Lu Feibohong, Wang Yunwu, Wang Boqi, Shi Zuicai (represented by Zhang Zhuping), Shen Huachen, Zhu Jingan, Wang Yaochen, etc.

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce should have a sincere love for industry and commerce. Shanghai is one of China's major commercial ports. Your association is located in such a large port, and you should be able to seek considerable happiness for industry and commerce. China is currently suffering the most from two things. Your association is organized by industrial and commercial groups across the country and public opinion circles such as Shen and Xin newspapers. In the future, you should be able to eliminate the pain of industry and commerce. The second is the issue of labor-capital disputes. I hope that everyone can find a way to properly maintain the original industry. Then, the Chinese industrial and commercial circles have great hope, etc. Next, Lin Kanghou gave a speech, saying that the past Chinese industry and commerce can be said to be (a dumb person eating coptis) with the pain of not being able to say anything. Today, I want to change this to (a dumb person eating sugar), which means that I hope the General Federation of Industries will change the (coptis) eaten by industry and commerce into (sugar). If so, the mission of the General Federation of Industries can be said to be great. Finally, the chairman replied, saying that all the gentlemen present are now members of this association. I am very honored to be sent to the venue by the Director of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for training. I would like to represent all the members to thank Director Zhao of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and sincerely hope that Director Zhao will assist the development of this association in the future with his industrial and commercial experience and knowledge in various tasks and affairs of this association, etc.

Inauguration Oath I swear to follow the Three Principles of the People and the teachings of the late Premier with sincerity, and to build the country for the national industry and create happiness for all members. I hereby swear.

Silk Factory Dispute Resolved Through Mediation 148

Labor and capital signed an agreement yesterday

Workers' wages are calculated at 58

The labor-capital dispute in the city's silk factory was caused by the capital side's regret the day before yesterday and refused the workers' request to calculate wages at 85% discount. After the Social Bureau repeatedly persuaded, the capital side expressed its concession and respected the intention of the Social Bureau. Yesterday afternoon, the mediation conditions have been signed. The situation yesterday is divided into the following:

At the mediation meeting at 4 pm yesterday, the capital side arrived representatives Shen Huachen and Zhang Peishen, and the labor side representatives Yu Fengtai, Chen Xiupu, Yu Qinbang, Yao Zilan, Xi Duan, Sun Dongkun, Wang Jianhao, Xu Pengnian, etc. Eight people gathered at the Social Bureau and were led into the mediation room by the bureau representative Qi Bing. At that time, both parties had expressed that there were no objections to the articles of the draft agreement the day before yesterday. However, the draft agreement ordered the day before yesterday was four articles. In order to prevent problems in the Shuang Gong Silk Factory, two articles were added yesterday, and both parties held a signing ceremony. Then, Wang Bing of the Social Bureau stood up and said to the labor side that the labor-capital dispute between the two parties has been resolved. In the future, I hope that the labor-capital parties will cooperate sincerely and help each other to prevent similar incidents from happening again. This time, the capital side representative Mr. Shen has made great efforts for this matter, and it is not easy to travel back and forth. In the future, workers should express their gratitude to Mr. Sun, etc. Next, the labor side expressed its gratitude to the Social Bureau. Finally, the labor side representative proposed that although the worker Chen Zhongxiang in Yichang has been released, he has been expelled. He requested that the capital side request the same industry association to send a letter to Yichang requesting reinstatement. The Social Bureau considered this to be another issue and will discuss it again.

Signing Conditions (1) The wages of all silk factory employees in Shanghai will be temporarily calculated at 85% discount of the original amount in each factory. (2) The silkworm moth subsidy obtained by the employees shall still be paid at 45% of the original salary. (3) The application work and other benefits that employees should receive shall still be in accordance with the old practice. (4) When the factory's business improves, the labor side may apply to restore the original wages, but the period of wage reduction shall be delayed until the end of May next year. (5) The treatment of employees in Shuang Gong Factory is different from that in Dan Gong Factory. If there are any changes, they must be submitted to the government for approval separately. (6) This agreement shall take effect from November.

Resumption of work The silk market in silk factories has slightly improved recently, and factories have resumed work one after another. According to a survey yesterday, 36 factories have resumed work. The special zone has Lunxiang, Yonglun, Xuxing, Yichang, Xukang, Xinchang, Dingyuan, Ruihe, Xiacheng, and Lunyuan. Ten factories in the West District include Shunfeng Yongxie An, Yong An, Qichang, Dingchang Sheng, Hengchang Xin, Fuchang Sheng, Fuchang Tai, Baisi First, Baisi Second, Hengkang, Fumin, Xiexing, Xiechang, Fengtai, Lichang, Yongchang, Feng Eighteen factories including etc. There are four factories in the North District: Yingfeng, Dalun, Jintai, and Fushen. There are four factories in the East District: Tianchang, Ruilun, Dingchang Xin, and Baokang. Four or five factories are expected to open today, etc.

All households that pay before the 18th will be issued customs duties treasury bonds, and those that pay after that will be given post-war treasury bonds. The Ministry of Finance's Fundraising Committee issued an important notice saying that the association has been fundraising for the 19th year customs duties short-term treasury bonds. All commercial and wealthy households in Shanghai have already been sent letters of encouragement. After investigation, it has been found that there are many households that are enthusiastically competing to purchase and pay in full, but there are also quite a few who delay watching or deliberately shirk. It must be known that the amount of fundraising determined by the ministry is divided into five grades based on the circumstances of each business, all of which are the lowest limit. The wealthy households are also only based on the standard of 40% of the actual payment of the first two-five treasury bonds. Households that pay before November 18th of the 19th year will be issued short-term treasury bonds for the 19th year customs duties treasury bonds. Those who pay after the 18th have also been instructed to change to short-term treasury bonds for the 19th year post-war treasury bonds. The stability of the treasury bond fund and the superior interest are exactly the same as the short-term treasury bonds for the 19th year customs duties treasury bonds, and there is no difference. It is hoped that each household will check the previous notices from the Ministry of Finance and the association and pay the full amount on the day designated by the Central China Communications Bank for collection so as to fill in the subscription bonds and exchange for treasury bonds at any time. I hope not to delay any longer. This is a special notice.
